[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Äì The stack trace is dominated by repeated invocations of [0m                        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m‚Ä¢ Vulnerability type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Äì The issue corresponds to a regex‚Äêbased denial‚Äêof‚Äêservice [0m[1;39m([0m[39mReDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m condition: [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcertain crafted input causes catastrophic backtracking in `java.util.regex.Pattern`[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m‚Ä¢ Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Äì The trace suggests deeply nested or overlapping quantifiers/groups that trigger[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ‚Äì The exception recommends reproducing with a reduced stack size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-Xss921k`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
